      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 22nd century
       </b>
       . During the period 2101 to 2200 there will be 235
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 79 will be partial, 87 will be annular (five
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 65 will be total, and 4 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be four, in 11 different years: 2112, 2134, 2141, 2152, 2159, 2170, 2177, 2181, 2188, 2195, and 2199.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
